ummary of Heat Exchanger Maximum Allowable Working Pressures :
N
ote: 
For Exchanger designs, the following values include MAWPs that 
consider the tubesheet, tubes, tube/tubesheet joint etc. These 
values were determined by iteration. Review the tubesheet analysis 
report for more information. 
 
Shell Side MAWP = 369.432 psig 
 Shell Side MAPnc = 429.561 psig 
 Channel Side MAWP = 364.926 psig 
 Channel Side MAPnc = 474.333 psig 
Internal Pressure Calculation Results :
A
SME Code, Section VIII Division 2 Class 2, 2017
Spherical Head From 10 To 20 SA-533 B , Fig. 3.8 Curve at 750 °F
S
pherical Shell Calculation - Section 4.3.5.1
C
omputed Minimum Required Thickness [t]: 
 = D/2*( exp( 0.5P/(S*E) )-1) + ci + co 
 = 86.116/2*(exp( 0.5 * 322.521/(37195.203*1.0))-1) + 0.125 + 0.0 
 = 0.1871 + 0.125 + 0.0 = 0.3121 in. 
C
omputed Maximum Allowable Working Pressure [MAWP]: 
 = 2 * S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) - Pliq 
 = 2 * 37195.2 * 1.0 * Ln( ( 2* 0.662 + 86.116 )/86.116 ) - 2.521 
 = 1135.705 - 2.521 = 1133.1838 psig 
C
omputed Maximum Allowable Pressure New & Cold [MAPnc]: 
 = 2 * S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) 
 = 2 * 37500.0 * 1.0 * Ln( ( 2* 0.787 + 85.866 )/85.866 ) 
 = 1363.0558 psig 
C
omputed Stress Intensity at Design Pressure [S]: 
 = P * D^2 / ( E( Do^2 - D^2 ) ) 
 = 322.521 * 86.116^2/( 1.0( 87.441^2 - 86.116^2 ) ) 
 = 10402.379 psi

C
ylindrical Shell Calculation - Section 4.3.3.1
C
omputed Minimum Required Thickness [t]: 
 = 0.5*D*( exp( P/(S*E) )-1)+ci+co 
 = 0.5*85.093*(exp( 325.845/(37195.203*1.0))-1) + 0.125 + 0.0 
 = 0.3744 + 0.125 + 0.0 = 0.4994 in. Equation 4.3.1 
C
omputed Maximum Allowable Working Pressure [MAWP]: 
 = S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) - Pliq 
 = 37195.203 * 1.0 * Ln( ( 2* 0.741 + 85.093 )/85.093 ) - 5.845 
 = 642.35 - 5.845 = 636.5054 psig 
C
omputed Maximum Allowable Pressure New & Cold [MAPnc]: 
 = S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) 
 = 37500.0 * 1.0 * Ln( ( 2* 0.866 + 84.843 )/84.843 ) 
 = 757.9516 psig 
C
omputed Stress Intensity at Design Pressure [S]: 
 = P * D / ( E( Do - D ) ) 
 = 325.845 * 85.093/( 1.0( 86.575 - 85.093 ) ) 
 = 18705.5703 psi 
P
ercent Fiber Elongation per Table 6.1
 
Cylinders formed from Plate (50*tnom/Rf)*(1-Rf/Ro) 1.011 %

ylindrical Shell Calculation - Section 4.3.3.1

omputed Maximum Allowable Working Pressure [MAWP]:

Elliptical Head From 40 To 50 SA-533 B , Fig. 3.8 Curve at 750 °F
H
ead Calculation - Section 4.3.6 (and Section 4.3.7 for Ellipsoidal Head)
C
omputed Minimum Required Thickness [t]: 
 tr = 0.3357 in. 
 t = tr + ci + co 
 = 0.3357 + 0.125 + 0.0 
 = 0.4607 in. - see below for the derivation 
F
or Elliptical heads: Compute [h, k, r,] per 4.3.7.1 and PTB-3 
 h = D/(2*Aspect Ratio) 
 = 84.843/(2*2.0) 
 = 21.211 in. 
 
k = D/(2*h) 
 = 84.843/(2*21.211) 
 = 2.000 
 
r = D( 0.5/k - 0.08 ) + ca 
 = 84.843( 0.5/2.0 - 0.08 ) + 0.125 
 = 14.548 in. 
 
L = D(0.44 * k + 0.02 ) + ca 
 = 84.843(0.44 *2.0 + 0.02) + 0.125 
 = 76.483 in. 
S
tep 3: Geometric Constants [BetaTh, PhiTh, Rth]: 
 Equations 4.3.8 to 4.3.11 as appropriate 
 t (corroded) and P for the calc.: t = 0.3357in. P = 325.8451 psig 
 
BetTh = acos[(0.5 * D - r)/(L - r)] 
= acos[(0.5 * 85.093 - 14.548)/(76.483 - 14.548)] 
= 1.1017 radians - Equation 4.3.8 
 
PhiTh = sqrt( L * t ) / r 
= sqrt( 76.483 * 0.336 )/14.548 
= 0.3483 radians - Equation 4.3.9 
 
PhiTh < BetaTh, Thus: 
 Rth = ( 0.5 * D - r ) / cos( BetaTh - PhiTh ) + r 
= ( 0.5 * 85.093 - 14.548 )/cos( 1.102 - 0.348 ) + 14.548 
= 52.9353 in. - Equation 4.3.10 
S
tep 4: Coefficients: Equations 4.3.12 to 4.3.15 [C1 and C2]: 
 r/D > 0.08, Thus: 
 C1 = 0.692 * ( r / D ) + 0.605 
 = 0.692 * ( 14.548/85.093 ) + 0.605 
 = 0.7233 - Equation 4.3.13 
 
C2 = 1.46 - 2.6 * ( r/D ) = 1.46 - 2.6 * ( 14.548/85.093 ) 
 = 1.0155 - Equation 4.3.15 
S
tep 5: Pressure to produce knuckle elastic buckling [Peth]:
 = C1 * Et * t² / ( C2 * Rth * ( 0.5 * Rth - r )) 
 = 0.723 * 24597198 * 0.336²/ 
 ( 1.015 * 52.935 * ( 0.5 * 52.935 - 14.548 )) 
 = 3130.16 psig - Equation 4.3.16 

[page 9]
PV Elite 2018 SP2 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 1950201-CAL-001-00
Internal Pressure Cal
culations: 
4 
S
tep 6: Internal Pressure for max stress in knuckle equals yield [Py]: 
 C3 = Sy = 55693.602 psi (Not in the creep range - 4.3.6.1(f) ) 
 
Py = C3 * t / ( C2 * Rth * ( 0.5 * Rth / r - 1 ) ) 
 = 55693.602* 0.336/(1.015* 52.935 * ( 0.5 * 52.935/14.548 - 1 )) 
 = 424.578 psig - Equation 4.3.17 
S
tep 7: Value of Internal Press. resulting in buckling of knuckle [G and Pck]: 
 G = Peth/Py = 3130.156/424.578 = 7.372 
 
G > 1, Thus: 
 Pck = ( ( 0.77508G - 0.20354G² + 0.019274*G³ ) / 
( 1 + 0.19014G - 0.089534G² + 0.0093965*G³ ) )Py 
= ( ( 0.77508*7.372-0.20354*7.372²+0.019274*7.372³)/ 
( 1+0.19014*7.372-0.089534*7.372²+0.0093965*7.372³))*424.578 
= 775.14 psig - Equation 4.3.19 
S
tep 8: Compute Allowable Pressure base on buckling of knuckle [Pak]: 
 = Pck/1.5 = 775.14/1.5 = 516.76 psig - Equation 4.3.21 
S
tep 9: Compute allowable pressure based on rupture of crown [Pac]: 
 = 2 * S * E / (L / t + 0.5 ) 
 = 2 * 37195.203 * 1.0/(76.483/0.336 + 0.5 ) 
 = 325.85 psig - Equation 4.3.22 
S
tep 10: Compute final pressure [Pa]: 
 = min( Pak, Pac ) = min(516.759, 325.845) 
 = 325.85 psig - Equation 4.3.23: (same as original design pressure) 
A
llowable pressure in Crown at given thickness [Pac]: 
 = 2 * S * E / (L / t + 0.5 ) 
 = 2 * 37195.203 * 1.0/(76.483/0.387 + 0.5 ) 
 = 375.277 psig 
C
omputed Maximum Allowable Pressure [MAWP]: 
 = MaxPressure - Pliq = 375.2775 - 5.845 = 369.4324 psig 
C
omputed Maximum Allowable Pressure New and Cold [MAPnc]: 
 = 501.0277 psig 
C
omputed Membrane Stress Intensity at Design Pressure [Sm]: 
 = 32295.766 psi

equired Thickness of Straight Flange = 0.499 in.

Spherical Head From Tsht to 20 Ext. Chart: CS-5 at 750 °F 
 
Maximum External Pressure per Code Case 2286 or Div. 2 Section 4.4 
 
Elastic Hoop Compressive Membrane Failure Stress [Fhe]: 
 = 0.075 * Ey * ( t / Ro ) 
 = 0.075 * 24597198 * ( 0.662/43.72 ) 
 = 27950.102 psi 
 
Ratio of Elastic Hoop Compressive Membrane Failure Stress to Yield [Fr]: 
 = Fhe / Sy 
 = 27950.1 / 55693.6 
 = 0.502 
 
Predicted Buckling Stress [Fic]: 
 Since Fr <= 0.55, Fic = Fhe 
 = 27950.102 psi

Allowable Circumferential Compressive Stress [Fha]: 
 Since Fr <= 0.55, Fha = Fhe/FS 
 = 27950.1/2.035 
 = 13733.845 psi 
 
Allowable External Pressure at the given Thickness [Pa]: 
 = 2 * Fha[t/Ro] 
 = 2 * 13733.845[ 0.662/43.72] 
 = 416.158 psig 
 
Cylindrical Shell From 20 to 30 Ext. Chart: CS-5 at 750 °F 
 
Maximum External Pressure per Code Case 2286 or Div. 2 Section 4.4 
 
Determine Parameter [Mx]: 
 = L / sqrt( Ro * t ) 
 = 240.158/sqrt( 43.287 * 0.741 ) 
 = 42.400 
 
Compute the Factor [Ch]: 
 Since Mx > 13 and Mx < 2 * (Do/t)0.94, Ch = 1.12 * Mx-1.058 
 = 1.12 * 42.4-1.058 
 = 0.0213 
 
Elastic Hoop Compressive Membrane Failure Stress [Fhe]: 
 = 1.6 * Ch * Ey * ( t / Do ) 
 = 1.6 * 0.021 * 24597198 * ( 0.741/86.575 ) 
 = 7161.130 psi 
 
Ratio of Elastic Hoop Compressive Membrane Failure Stress to Yield [Fr]: 
 = Fhe / Fy 
 = 7161.1/55693.6 
 = 0.129 
 
Predicted Buckling Stress [Fic]: 
 Since Fr <= 0.552, Fic = Fhe 
 = 7161.130 psi 
 
Factor of Safety [FS]: 
 Since Fic [7161.13] < 0.55 * 55693.6, FS = 2 
 
Allowable Circumferential Compressive Stress [Fha]: 
 Since Fr <= 0.552, Fha = Fhe/FS 
 = 7161.130/2.000 
 = 3580.565 psi 
 
Allowable External Pressure at the given Thickness [Pa]: 
 = 2 * Fha * ( t / Do ) 
 = 2 * 3580.565 * ( 0.741/86.575 ) 
 = 61.304 psig 
 
Cylindrical Shell From 30 to Ring_Pext Ext. Chart: CS-5 at 750 °F 
 
Maximum External Pressure per Code Case 2286 or Div. 2 Section 4.4 
 
Determine Parameter [Mx]: 
 = L / sqrt( Ro * t ) 
 = 240.158/sqrt( 43.012 * 0.466 ) 
 = 53.668 
 
Compute the Factor [Ch]: 
 Since Mx > 13 and Mx < 2 * (Do/t)0.94, Ch = 1.12 * Mx-1.058 
 = 1.12 * 53.668-1.058 
 = 0.0166

Minimum Required Thickness for Shear [HreqS]: 
 = 1/(4 * Mu) * (Do/(0.8 * S)) * [Ps - Pt] + Cats + Catc 
 = 1/(4 * 0.286 ) * (83.03/(0.8 * 26496.8 )) * [-15.0 - 320.0 ] + 0.25 
 = 1.3982 in. 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 1: 
 
Compute the Equivalent Outer Tube Limit Circle Diameter [Do]: 
 = 2 * ro + dt 
 = 2 * 41.2032 + 0.625 = 83.031 in. 
 
Determine the Basic Ligament Efficiency for Shear [mu]: 
 = (p - dt) / p 
 = ( 0.875 - 0.625 )/0.875 = 0.286 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 2: 
 
Compute the Ratio [Rhos]: 
 = Ds / Do (Configurations a, b, c) 
 = 85.0925/83.0314 = 1.0248 
 
Compute the Ratio [Rhoc]: 
 = Dc / Do (Configurations a, e, f) 
 = 86.1161/83.0314 = 1.0372 
 
Moment on Tubesheet due to Pressures (Ps, Pt) [Mts]: 
 = Do²/16 * [(Rhos-1)*(Rhos²+1)* Ps - (Rhoc-1) * (Rhoc²+1) * Pt ] 
 = 83.031²/16 * [ (1.025 - 1) * (1.025² + 1) * -14.997 - 
 (1.037 - 1) * (1.037² + 1) * 320.0 ] 
 = -10961.7852 psig*in.² 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 3: 
 
Compute the Ratio [rho]: 
 = ltx/h = 0.0/6.4429 = 0.0 ( must be 0 <= rho <= 1 ) 
 
Compute the Effective Tube Hole Diameter [d*]: 
 = max( dt - 2tt*( Et/E )( St/S )( rho ), dt - 2tt) 
 = max( 0.625 -2* 0.065 *(24847414/24248608 )* 
 ( 13889/26496 )*(0.0 ), 0.625 -2* 0.065 ) 
 = 0.6250 in. 
 
Compute the Effective Tube Pitch [p*]: 
 = p / sqrt( 1 - 4 * min( AL * CNV_factor, 4*Do*p)/(Pi * Do²) ) 
 = 0.875/sqrt( 1 - 4 * min( 290.94 *1.0, 4*83.031 * 0.875 ) 
 (3.141* 83.031²) ) 
 = 0.8995 in. 
 
Compute the Effective Ligament Efficiency for Bending [mu*]: 
 = (p* - d*)/p* = ( 0.8995 - 0.625 )/0.8995 = 0.30515 
 
E*/E, nu* for Triangular pattern from Div. 2 Tables 5.E.1, 5.E.2. 
 h/p = 7.363326 ; mu* = 0.305147 
 E*/E = 0.287905 ; nu* = 0.350376 ; E* = 6981298. psi 
 
Note: As h/p (7.363) is > 2, data values for h/p = 2 were used. 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 4: 
 
Compute Shell Coefficient [betaS]: 
 = (( 12 * (1-nus²))^0.25 )/((Ds + ts) * ts )½ 
 = (( 12 * (1 - 0.3²) )^0.25 )/(( 85.0925 + 0.7411 ) * 0.7411 )½ 
 = 0.2279 1/in. 
 
Determine Shell Coefficient [ks]:

PV Elite 2018 SP2 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L.

 = betaS * Es * ts³ / ( 6 * (1 - rnus²) ) 
 = 0.228 * 24597214 * 0.741³/( 6 * (1 - 0.3²) ) 
 = 417997.1250 psig*in.² 
 
Determine Shell Coefficient [Lambdas]: 
 = (6*Ds*ks)/h³ * (1 + h*betaS + *(h*betaS)²/2 ) 
 = 6* 85.093 * 417997.125/6.443³ * ( 1 + 6.443 * 0.228 + 1.078 ) 
 = 2829983.0000 psig 
 
Determine Shell Coefficient [deltaS]: 
 = Ds²/(4 * Es * Ts) * ( 1 - nus/2 ) 
 = 85.093²/( 4 * 24597214 * 0.741 ) * ( 1 - 0.3/2 ) 
 = 0.0000844023 in./psi 
 
Calculate Parameter [OmegaS]: 
 = rhos * ks * betaS * deltaS( 1 + h * betaS ) 
 = 1.0248 * 417997.12 * 0.2279 * 0.844E-04 ( 1 + 6.4429 * 0.2279 ) 
 = 20.3412 in.² 
 
Determine Channel Coefficient [betac]: 
 = (( 12 * (1 - nuc²) )^0.25 )/((Dc + tc) * tc )^0.5 
 = (( 12 * (1 - 0.3²) )^0.25 )/((86.1161 + 0.6624 ) * 0.6624 )^0.5 
 = 0.2398 1/in. 
 
Determine Channel Coefficient [kc]: 
 = betac * Ec * tc³ / ( 6 * (1 - rnus²) ) 
 = 0.24 * 24597214 * 0.662³/( 6 * (1 - 0.3²) ) 
 = 313939.5938 psig*in.² 
 
Determine Channel Coefficient [Lambdac]: 
 = (6*Dc*kc)/h³ * (1 + h*betac + (h*betac)²/2) 
 = 6*86.116 *313939.594/(6.443³) * ( 1 + 6.443 * 0.24 + 1.193 ) 
 = 2267117.0000 psig 
 
Determine Channel Coefficient [deltaC]: 
 = Dc²/(4 * Ec * Tc) * ( 1 - nuc )/2 
 = 86.116²/( 4 * 24597214 * 0.662 ) * ( 1 - 0.3 )/2 
 = 0.0000398263 in./psi 
 
Calculate Parameter [OmegaC]: 
 = rhoc * kc * Betac * deltaC( 1 + h * betac ) 
 = 1.0372 * 313939.59 * 0.2398 * 0.398E-04 ( 1 + 6.4429 * 0.2398 ) 
 = 7.9122 in.²

Results for ASME U-tube Tubesheet Calculations for Configuration a, 
Per Edition 2017, Original Thickness : 
 
Minimum Required Thickness for Shear [HreqS]: 
 = 1/(4 * Mu) * (Do/(0.8 * S)) * [Ps - Pt] + Cats + Catc 
 = 1/(4 * 0.286 ) * (83.03/(0.8 * 26496.8 )) * [320.0 - -15.0 ] + 0.25 
 = 1.3982 in. 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 1: 
 
Compute the Equivalent Outer Tube Limit Circle Diameter [Do]: 
 = 2 * ro + dt 
 = 2 * 41.2032 + 0.625 = 83.031 in. 
 
Determine the Basic Ligament Efficiency for Shear [mu]: 
 = (p - dt) / p 
 = ( 0.875 - 0.625 )/0.875 = 0.286 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 2: 
 
Compute the Ratio [Rhos]: 
 = Ds / Do (Configurations a, b, c) 
 = 85.0925/83.0314 = 1.0248 
 
Compute the Ratio [Rhoc]: 
 = Dc / Do (Configurations a, e, f) 
 = 86.1161/83.0314 = 1.0372 
 
Moment on Tubesheet due to Pressures (Ps, Pt) [Mts]: 
 = Do²/16 * [(Rhos-1)*(Rhos²+1)* Ps - (Rhoc-1) * (Rhoc²+1) * Pt ] 
 = 83.031²/16 * [ (1.025 - 1) * (1.025² + 1) * 320.0 - 

[page 23]
PV Elite 2018 SP2 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 1950201-CAL-001-00 
ASME TS Calc: tsh 
 
18 
 (1.037 - 1) * (1.037² + 1) * -14.997 ] 
 = 7515.8843 psig*in.² 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 3: 
 
Compute the Ratio [rho]: 
 = ltx/h = 0.0/6.4429 = 0.0 ( must be 0 <= rho <= 1 ) 
 
Compute the Effective Tube Hole Diameter [d*]: 
 = max( dt - 2tt*( Et/E )( St/S )( rho ), dt - 2tt) 
 = max( 0.625 -2* 0.065 *(24847414/24248608 )* 
 ( 13889/26496 )*(0.0 ), 0.625 -2* 0.065 ) 
 = 0.6250 in. 
 
Compute the Effective Tube Pitch [p*]: 
 = p / sqrt( 1 - 4 * min( AL * CNV_factor, 4*Do*p)/(Pi * Do²) ) 
 = 0.875/sqrt( 1 - 4 * min( 290.94 *1.0, 4*83.031 * 0.875 ) 
 (3.141* 83.031²) ) 
 = 0.8995 in. 
 
Compute the Effective Ligament Efficiency for Bending [mu*]: 
 = (p* - d*)/p* = ( 0.8995 - 0.625 )/0.8995 = 0.30515 
 
E*/E, nu* for Triangular pattern from Div. 2 Tables 5.E.1, 5.E.2. 
 h/p = 7.363326 ; mu* = 0.305147 
 E*/E = 0.287905 ; nu* = 0.350376 ; E* = 6981298. psi 
 
Note: As h/p (7.363) is > 2, data values for h/p = 2 were used. 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 4: 
 
Compute Shell Coefficient [betaS]: 
 = (( 12 * (1-nus²))^0.25 )/((Ds + ts) * ts )½ 
 = (( 12 * (1 - 0.3²) )^0.25 )/(( 85.0925 + 0.7411 ) * 0.7411 )½ 
 = 0.2279 1/in. 
 
Determine Shell Coefficient [ks]: 
 = betaS * Es * ts³ / ( 6 * (1 - rnus²) ) 
 = 0.228 * 24597214 * 0.741³/( 6 * (1 - 0.3²) ) 
 = 417997.1250 psig*in.² 
 
Determine Shell Coefficient [Lambdas]: 
 = (6*Ds*ks)/h³ * (1 + h*betaS + *(h*betaS)²/2 ) 
 = 6* 85.093 * 417997.125/6.443³ * ( 1 + 6.443 * 0.228 + 1.078 ) 
 = 2829983.0000 psig 
 
Determine Shell Coefficient [deltaS]: 
 = Ds²/(4 * Es * Ts) * ( 1 - nus/2 ) 
 = 85.093²/( 4 * 24597214 * 0.741 ) * ( 1 - 0.3/2 ) 
 = 0.0000844023 in./psi 
 
Calculate Parameter [OmegaS]: 
 = rhos * ks * betaS * deltaS( 1 + h * betaS ) 
 = 1.0248 * 417997.12 * 0.2279 * 0.844E-04 ( 1 + 6.4429 * 0.2279 ) 
 = 20.3412 in.² 
 
Determine Channel Coefficient [betac]: 
 = (( 12 * (1 - nuc²) )^0.25 )/((Dc + tc) * tc )^0.5 
 = (( 12 * (1 - 0.3²) )^0.25 )/((86.1161 + 0.6624 ) * 0.6624 )^0.5 
 = 0.2398 1/in. 
 
Determine Channel Coefficient [kc]: 
 = betac * Ec * tc³ / ( 6 * (1 - rnus²) ) 
 = 0.24 * 24597214 * 0.662³/( 6 * (1 - 0.3²) ) 
 = 313939.5938 psig*in.²

Determine Channel Coefficient [Lambdac]: 
 = (6*Dc*kc)/h³ * (1 + h*betac + (h*betac)²/2) 
 = 6*86.116 *313939.594/(6.443³) * ( 1 + 6.443 * 0.24 + 1.193 ) 
 = 2267117.0000 psig 
 
Determine Channel Coefficient [deltaC]: 
 = Dc²/(4 * Ec * Tc) * ( 1 - nuc )/2 
 = 86.116²/( 4 * 24597214 * 0.662 ) * ( 1 - 0.3 )/2 
 = 0.0000398263 in./psi 
 
Calculate Parameter [OmegaC]: 
 = rhoc * kc * Betac * deltaC( 1 + h * betac ) 
 = 1.0372 * 313939.59 * 0.2398 * 0.398E-04 ( 1 + 6.4429 * 0.2398 ) 
 = 7.9122 in.² 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 5: 
 
Diameter ratio [K]: 
 = A/Do = 87.4409/83.0314 = 1.0531 
 
Determine Coefficient [F]: 
 = (1 - nu*)/E* * ( Lambdas + Lambdac + E * ln(K) ) 
 = (1 - 0.35 )/6981298 * ( 2829983 + 2267117 + 
 24248608 * ln(1.05 ) ) 
 = 0.5911 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 6: 
 
Moment Acting on Unperforated Tubesheet Rim [M*] 
 = Mts + OmegaC * Pt - OmegaS * Ps 
 = 7515.884 + 7.912 * -14.997 - 20.341 * 320.0 
 = 888.0327 psig*in.² 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 7: 
 
Maximum Bending Moment acting on Periphery of Tubesheet [Mp]: 
 = ((M*) - Do²/32 * F * (Ps - Pt) ) / (1 + F) 
 = ((888.03 ) - 83.031²/32 * 0.591 * (320.0 - -15.0 ) )/(1 + 0.59 ) 
 = -26253.0938 psig*in.² 
 
Maximum Bending Moment acting on Center of Tubesheet [Mo]: 
 = Mp + Do²/64 * (3 + rnu*)(Ps - Pt) 
 = -26253.09 + 83.031²/64 * (3 + 0.35 )(320.0 - -15.0 ) 
 = 94650.5938 psig*in.² 
 
Maximum Bending Moment acting on Tubesheet [M]: 
 = Max( abs(Mp), abs(Mo) ) 
 = Max( abs(-26253.094), abs(94650.594 ) ) 
 = 94650.5938 psig*in.² 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 8: 
 
Tubesheet Bending Stress at Original Thickness: 
 = 6 * M / ( (mu*) * ( h - hg')² ) 
 = 6 * 94650.594/( ( 0.3051 ) * ( 6.4429 - 0.0 )² ) 
 = 44833.4141 psi 
 
The Allowable Tubesheet Bending Stress [SigmaAll]: 
 = 2 * S = 2 * 26496.8 = 52993.6 psi 
 
Tubesheet Bending Stress at Final Thickness [Sigma]: 
 = 6 * M / ( (mu*) * ( h - hg')² 
 = 6 * 92171.82/( ( 0.3051 ) * ( 5.8581 - 0.0 )² 
 = 52811.8359 psi

 abs(Ps - Pt) = abs(320.0 - -15.0 ) = 334.997 psig

 = 3.2 * S * MU * h / Do

 = 3777.54 psi 
 
ASME Section VIII-2 Part 4.18.7.4 Step 10: 
 
Axial Shell Membrane Stress [Sigmasm]: 
 = Ds² / (4 * ts * (Ds + ts) ) * Ps 
 = 85.0925²/(4 * 0.7411 * (85.0925 + 0.7411 ) ) * 320.0 
 = 9105.711 psi 
 
Axial Shell Bending Stress [Sigmasb]: 
 = 6*ks/ts² * ( betaS * P's + 6*(1 - rnu*) / (E*) * 
 Do/h³ * (1 + h * betaS/2) * (Mp + Do² / 32 * (Ps - Pt) )) 
 = 6*417997.12/0.741² * [ 0.228 * 0.03 + 6*(1 - 0.35 )/6981298 * 
 83.031/6.443³ * (1 + 6.443 * 0.228/2) *(-26253.09 + 83.031²/32 * 
 (320.0 - -15.0 )) ] 
 = 91129.906 psi 
 
Shell Membrane + Bending Stress [Sigmas]: 
 = abs(Sigma_sm) + abs(Sigma_sb) (Should be <= 1.5*Ss) 
 = 100235.617 psi (Should be <= 55792.84) 
 
Axial Channel Membrane Stress [Sigmacm]: 
 = Dc² / (4 * tc * (Dc + tc) ) * Pt 
 = 86.1161²/(4 * 0.6624 * (86.1161 + 0.6624 ) ) * -14.997 
 = -483.712 psi 
 
Axial Channel Bending Stress [Sigmacb]: 
 = 6*kc/tc² * [ Betac * (deltaC*Pt) - 6*(1 - nu*) / (E*) * 
 Do/h³ * (1 + h * Betac/2) * (Mp + Do²/32 * (Ps-Pt)) ] 
 = 6*313939.59/0.662² * [ 0.24 * -0.0 - 6*(1 - 0.35 )/6981298 * 
 83.031/6.443³ * (1 + 6.443 * 0.24/2) *(-26253.09 + 83.031²/32 * 
 (320.0 - -15.0 )) ] 
 = -61175.688 psi 
 
Channel Membrane + Bending Stress [Sigmac]: 
 = abs(Sigmacm) + abs(Sigmacb) (Should be <= 1.5*Sc) 
 = 61659.398 psi (Should be <= 55792.84)

 83.031/6.443³ * (1 + 6.443 * 0.228/2) *(-4772.07 + 83.031²/32 * 
 (320.0 - 320.0 )) ] 
 = 21556.746 psi 
 
Shell Membrane + Bending Stress [Sigmas]: 
 = abs(Sigma_sm) + abs(Sigma_sb) (Should be <= 1.5*Ss) 
 = 30662.457 psi (Should be <= 55792.84) 
 
Axial Channel Membrane Stress [Sigmacm]: 
 = Dc² / (4 * tc * (Dc + tc) ) * Pt 
 = 86.1161²/(4 * 0.6624 * (86.1161 + 0.6624 ) ) * 320.0 
 = 10321.086 psi 
 
Axial Channel Bending Stress [Sigmacb]: 
 = 6*kc/tc² * [ Betac * (deltaC*Pt) - 6*(1 - nu*) / (E*) * 
 Do/h³ * (1 + h * Betac/2) * (Mp + Do²/32 * (Ps-Pt)) ] 
 = 6*313939.59/0.662² * [ 0.24 * 0.01 - 6*(1 - 0.35 )/6981298 * 
 83.031/6.443³ * (1 + 6.443 * 0.24/2) *(-4772.07 + 83.031²/32 * 
 (320.0 - 320.0 )) ] 
 = 19411.428 psi 
 
Channel Membrane + Bending Stress [Sigmac]: 
 = abs(Sigmacm) + abs(Sigmacb) (Should be <= 1.5*Sc) 
 = 29732.514 psi (Should be <= 55792.84) 
 
 
Tube Weld Size Results per 4.18.10: 
 
Tube Strength [Ft]: 
 = 3.1415 * t * ( do - t ) * Sa 
 = 3.1415 * 0.065 * ( 0.625 - 0.065 ) * 13890.0 = 1588.377 lb. 
 
Fillet Weld Strength, Ff = 0.0 
 
Groove Weld Strength [Fg]: 
 = 0.85 * 3.1415 * ag * (do + 0.67*ag) * Sw (but not > Ft) 
 = 0.85 * 3.1415 * 0.065 * ( 0.625 + 0.67* 0.065 ) * 13890.0 
 = 1588.3766 lb. 
 
 Max. Allow. Tube-Tubesheet Joint load, Lmax 
 = Ft = 1588.3766 lb. 
 
Design Strength Ratio [fd]: 
 = 1.0000 
 
Weld Strength Factor [fw]: 
 = Sot / ( Min(Sot, S) ) = 1.0000 
 
Min Weld Length [ar]: 
 = ( (0.75 * do)² + 1.76*t*(do - t)* fw * fd ) )½ - 0.75 * do 
 = 0.0640 in.

 = 0.5*D*( exp( P/(S*E) )-1)+ci+co 
 = 0.5*24.25*(exp( 321.259/(26496.799*1.0))-1) + 0.125 + 0.0

 = S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) - Pliq 
 = 26496.799 * 1.0 * Ln( ( 2*2.867 + 24.25 )/24.25 ) - 0.0 
 = 5624.097 - 0.0 = 5624.0972 psig

Nozzle Material Factor [frn]: 
 = min[Sn/S, 1] 
 = min[26496.8/37195.2, 1] 
 = 0.712 
 
Thickness of Nozzle [tn]: 
 = thickness - corrosion allowance 
 = 2.992 - 0.125 
 = 2.867 in. 
 
Effective Pressure Radius [Reff]: 
 = Di/2 + corrosion allowance 
 = 85.866/2 + 0.125 
 = 43.058 in. 
 
Effective Length of Vessel Wall [LR]: 
 = min( sqrt( Reff * t ), 2 * Rn ) 
 = min( sqrt( 43.058 * 0.662 ), 2 * 12.125 ) 
 = 5.341 in. 
 
Intermediate value [Cn]: 
 = min( (( t + te )/tn)^0.35, 1 ) 
 = min( (( 0.662 + 0.0 )/2.867)^0.35, 1 ) 
 = min( 0.599, 1 ) 
 = 0.599 
 
Intermediate value [Cp]: 
 = 9999999.000 
 
Effective Nozzle Wall Length Outside the Vessel [LH]: 
 = min( t + te + Fp * sqrt( Rn*tn ), Lpr1 + t ) 
 = min(0.662+0.0+0.599*sqrt(12.125*2.867),3.15+0.662) 
 = 3.812 in. 
 
Effective Vessel Thickness [teff]: 
 = t + (( A5 * frp ) / LR ) 
 = 0.662+((0.0*1.0)/5.341) 
 = 0.662 in.

Area Contributed by the Vessel Wall [A1]: 
 = t * LR 
 = 0.662 * 5.341

 = 3.538 in²

Compute Areas A1-A43 (No Pad) or A1-A5 (With Pad) : 
 
Area Contributed by the Vessel Wall [A1]: 
 = t * LR 
 = 0.662 * 5.341

36 
 = 3.538 in² 
 
Area Contributed by the Nozzle Outside the Vessel Wall [A2]: 
 = tn * LH 
 = 0.843 * 3.481 
 = 2.935 in² 
 
Area Contributed by the Outside Fillet Weld [A41]: 
 = 0.5 * Leg412 
 = 0.5 * 0.3942 
 = 0.078 in² 
 
The total area contributed by A1 through A43 [AT]: 
 = A1 + frn( A2 + A3 ) + A41 + A42 + A43 
 = 3.538+0.398(2.935+0.0)+0.078+0.0+0.0 
 = 4.782 in² 
 
Nozzle Radius for Force Calculation [Rxn]: 
 = tn / ln[1 + tn/Rn ] 
 = 0.843/ln[ 1 + 0.843/11.157 ] 
 = 11.573 in. 
 
Shell Radius for Force Calculation [Rxs]: 
 = teff / ln[ 1 + teff/Reff ] 
 = 0.662/ln[ 1 + 0.662/43.058 ] 
 = 43.388 in. 
 
Allowable Local Primary Membrane Stress [Sallow]: 
 = 1.5 * S * E 
 = 1.5 * 37195.203 * 1.0 
 = 55792.8 psi 
 
Determine Force acting on the Nozzle [fN]: 
 = P * Rxn * LH 
 = 320.169 * 11.573 * 3.481 
 = 12898.8 lb. 
 
Determine Force acting on the Shell [fS]: 
 = P * Rxs * ( LR + tn )/2 
 = 320.169 * 43.388 * ( 5.341 + 0.843 )/2 
 = 42949.8 lb. 
 
Discontinuity Force from Internal Pressure [fY]: 
 = ( P * Rxs * Rnc )/2 
 = ( 320.169 * 43.388 * 11.157 )/2 
 = 77494.1 lb. 
 
Area Resisting Internal Pressure [Ap]: 
 = ( fS + fY + fN )/P 
 = ( 42949.8 + 77494.1 + 12898.8 )/320.169 
 = 416.5 in² 
 
Maximum Allowable Working Pressure Candidate [Pmax1]: 
 = Sallow /( 2 * Ap/AT - Rxs/(2 * teff ) ) 
 = 55792.805/( 2 * 416.476/4.782 - 43.388/(2* 0.662) ) 
 = 394.5 psig

 = 2 * S * [t/Rxs] 
 = 2 * 37195.203 * [ 0.662/43.388] 
 = 1135.7 psig

 = min( Pmax1, Pmax2 ) 
 = min( 394.465, 1135.705 ) 
 = 394.465 psig

 = 0.5*D*( exp( P/(S*E) )-1)+ci+co 
 = 0.5*22.314*(exp( 322.349/(14788.799*1.0))-1) + 0.125 + 0.0

Nozzle Calculations per Section 4.5: Internal Pressure Case: 
 
Nozzle Material Factor [frn]: 
 = min[Sn/S, 1] 
 = min[14788.8/37195.2, 1] 
 = 0.398 
 
Thickness of Nozzle [tn]: 
 = thickness - corrosion allowance 
 = 0.968 - 0.125 
 = 0.843 in. 
 
Effective Pressure Radius [Reff]: 
 = Di/2 + corrosion allowance 
 = 85.866/2 + 0.125 
 = 43.058 in. 
 
Effective Length of Vessel Wall [LR]: 
 = min( sqrt( Reff * t ), 2 * Rn ) 
 = min( sqrt( 43.058 * 0.662 ), 2 * 11.157 ) 
 = 5.341 in. 
 
Intermediate value [Cn]: 
 = min( (( t + te )/tn)^0.35, 1 ) 
 = min( (( 0.662 + 0.0 )/0.843)^0.35, 1 ) 
 = min( 0.919, 1 ) 
 = 0.919 
 
Intermediate value [Cp]: 
 = 9999999.000

 = min(0.662+0.0+0.919*sqrt(11.157*0.843),11.811+0.662) 
 = 3.481 in.

 = 0.662+((0.0*1.0)/5.341)

 = teff / ln[ 1 + teff/Reff ] 
 = 0.662/ln[ 1 + 0.662/43.058 ] 
 = 43.388 in. 
 
Allowable Local Primary Membrane Stress [Sallow]: 
 = Shell Fha Value 
 = 13733.845 
 = 13733.8 psi 
 
Determine Force acting on the Nozzle [fN]: 

[page 51]
PV Elite 2018 SP2 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 1950201-CAL-001-00 
Nozzle Calcs.: T2 
 
46 
 = P * Rxn * LH 
 = 14.997 * 11.573 * 3.481 
 = 604.2 lb. 
 
Determine Force acting on the Shell [fS]: 
 = P * Rxs * ( LR + tn )/2 
 = 14.997 * 43.388 * ( 5.341 + 0.843 )/2 
 = 2011.8 lb. 
 
Discontinuity Force from External Pressure [fY]: 
 = ( P * Rxs * Rnc )/2 
 = ( 14.997 * 43.388 * 11.157 )/2 
 = 3630.0 lb. 
 
Area Resisting External Pressure [Ap]: 
 = ( fS + fY + fN )/P 
 = ( 2011.8 + 3630.0 + 604.2 )/14.997 
 = 416.5 in² 
 
Maximum Allowable Working Pressure Candidate [Pmax1]: 
 = Sallow /( 2 * Ap/AT - Rxs/(2 * teff ) ) 
 = 13733.845/( 2 * 416.476/4.782 - 43.388/(2* 0.662) ) 
 = 97.1 psig 
 
Maximum Allowable Working Pressure Candidate [Pmax2]: 
 = 2 * Fha * [t/Rxs] 
 = 2 * 13733.845 * [ 0.662/43.388] 
 = 419.3 psig 
 
Maximum Allowable Working Pressure [Pmax]: 
 = min( Pmax1, Pmax2 ) 
 = min( 97.101, 419.344 ) 
 = 97.101 psig 
 
Average Primary Membrane Stress [SigmaAvg]: 
 = ( fN + fS + fY ) / AT 
 = ( 604.201 + 2011.841 + 3629.958 )/4.782 
 = 1306.184 psi 
 
General Primary Membrane Stress [SigmaCirc]: 
 = P * Rxs / ( 2 * teff ) 
 = 14.997 * 43.388/( 2 * 0.662 ) 
 = 491.2 psi 
 
Maximum Local Primary Membrane Stress [PL]: 
 = max( 2 * SigmaAvg - SigmaCirc, SigmaCirc ) 
 = max( 2 * 1306.184 - 491.171, 491.171 ) 
 = 2121.2 psi 
 
Summary of Nozzle Pressure/Stress Results: 
 Allowed Local Primary Membrane Stress Sallow 13733.84 psi 
 Local Primary Membrane Stress PL 2121.20 psi 
 Maximum Allowable External Pressure Pmax 97.10 psig

Cylindrical Shell Calculation - Section 4.3.3.1 
 
Computed Minimum Required Thickness [t]: 
 = 0.5*D*( exp( P/(S*E) )-1)+ci+co 
 = 0.5*20.626*(exp( 325.836/(14788.799*1.0))-1) + 0.125 + 0.0 
 = 0.2297 + 0.125 + 0.0 = 0.3547 in. Equation 4.3.1 
 
Computed Maximum Allowable Working Pressure [MAWP]: 
 = S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) - Pliq 
 = 14788.799 * 1.0 * Ln( ( 2*1.687 + 20.626 )/20.626 ) - 0.0 
 = 2240.524 - 0.0 = 2240.5237 psig 
 
Nozzle Minimum Thickness per Table 4.5.2 
 Min. required Nozzle Neck Thickness + c : 0.453 in. 11.515 mm 
 
Nozzle Calculations per Section 4.5: Internal Pressure Case: 
 
Nozzle Material Factor [frn]: 
 = min[Sn/S, 1] 
 = min[14788.8/37195.2, 1] 
 = 0.398 
 
Thickness of Nozzle [tn]: 
 = thickness - corrosion allowance 
 = 1.812 - 0.125 
 = 1.687 in. 
 
Shell Diameter to Thickness ratio [D/t]: 
 = Di/t 
 = 85.093/0.741 
 = 114.813 must be less than 400. 
 
Effective Pressure Radius [Reff]: 
 = Di/2 + corrosion allowance 
 = 84.843/2 + 0.125 
 = 42.546 in. 
 
Effective Length of Vessel Wall [LR]: 
 = min( sqrt( Reff * t ), 2 * Rn ) 
 = min( sqrt( 42.546 * 0.741 ), 2 * 10.313 ) 
 = 5.615 in. 
 
Thickness Limit Candidate [LH1]: 
 = min[1.5t,te] + sqrt( Rn * tn ) 
 = min[1.5* 0.741, 0.0] + sqrt( 10.313 * 1.687 ) 
 = 4.171 in. 
 
Thickness Limit Candidate [LH2]: 
 = Lpr1 
 = 11.811 
 = 11.811 in. 
 
Thickness Limit Candidate [LH3]: 
 = 8( t + te ) 
 = 8( 0.741 + 0.0 ) 
 = 5.929 in.

Effective Nozzle Wall Length Outside the Vessel [LH]: 
 = min[ LH1, LH2, LH3 ] + t for set-in nozzles 
 = min[ 4.171, 11.811, 5.929 ) + 0.741 
 = 4.912 in. 
 
Effective Vessel Thickness [teff]: 
 = t + (( A5 * frp ) / LR ) 
 = 0.741+((0.0*1.0)/5.615) 
 = 0.741 in. 
 
Determine Parameter [Lamda]: 
 = min( 12, ( 2*Rn + tn )/( sqrt( ( Di + teff ) * teff )) ) 
 = min( 12, (2*10.31 + 1.687)/( sqrt((85.09 + 0.741) * 0.741)) ) 
 = 2.798 
 
Compute Areas A1-A43 (No Pad) or A1-A5 (With Pad) : 
 
Area Contributed by the Vessel Wall [A1]: 
 = t * LR * max( (Lamda/5)0.85, 1 ) 
 = 0.741 * 5.615 * max( (2.798/5)0.85, 1 ) 
 = 4.162 in² 
 
Area Contributed by the Nozzle Outside the Vessel Wall [A2]: 
 = tn * LH 
 = 1.687 * 4.912 
 = 8.287 in² 
 
Area Contributed by the Outside Fillet Weld [A41]: 
 = 0.5 * Leg412 
 = 0.5 * 0.3942 
 = 0.078 in² 
 
The total area contributed by A1 through A43 [AT]: 
 = A1 + frn( A2 + A3 ) + A41 + A42 + A43 
 = 4.162+0.398(8.287+0.0)+0.078+0.0+0.0 
 = 7.534 in² 
 
Nozzle Radius for Force Calculation [Rxn]: 
 = tn / ln[1 + tn/Rn ] 
 = 1.687/ln[ 1 + 1.687/10.313 ] 
 = 11.135 in. 
 
Shell Radius for Force Calculation [Rxs]: 
 = teff / ln[ 1 + teff/Reff ] 
 = 0.741/ln[ 1 + 0.741/42.546 ] 
 = 42.916 in. 
 
Allowable Local Primary Membrane Stress [Sallow]: 
 = 1.5 * S * E 
 = 1.5 * 37195.203 * 1.0 
 = 55792.8 psi

 = P * Rxn * LH 
 = 325.836 * 11.135 * 4.912 
 = 17822.9 lb. 
 
Determine Force acting on the Shell [fS]: 
 = P * Rxs( LR + tn ) 
 = 325.836 * 42.916( 5.615 + 1.687 ) 
 = 102113.2 lb. 
 
Discontinuity Force from Internal Pressure [fY]: 
 = P * Rxs * Rnc 
 = 325.836 * 42.916 * 10.313 
 = 144211.8 lb.

Reinforcement CALCULATION, Description: S2 
 
ASME Code, Section VIII, Div. 2, 2017, Section 4.5.1 - 4.5.14 
 
 Actual Inside Diameter Used in Calculation 20.376 in. 
 Actual Thickness Used in Calculation 1.812 in. 
 
Nozzle input data check completed without errors. 
 
Cylindrical Shell Calculation - Section 4.3.3.1 
 
Computed Minimum Required Thickness [t]: 
 = 0.5*D*( exp( P/(S*E) )-1)+ci+co 
 = 0.5*20.626*(exp( 320.0/(14788.799*1.0))-1) + 0.125 + 0.0 
 = 0.2256 + 0.125 + 0.0 = 0.3506 in. Equation 4.3.1 
 
Computed Maximum Allowable Working Pressure [MAWP]: 
 = S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) - Pliq 
 = 14788.799 * 1.0 * Ln( ( 2*1.687 + 20.626 )/20.626 ) - 0.0 
 = 2240.524 - 0.0 = 2240.5237 psig 
 
Nozzle Minimum Thickness per Table 4.5.2 
 Min. required Nozzle Neck Thickness + c : 0.453 in. 11.515 mm 
 
 
Nozzle Calculations per Section 4.5: Internal Pressure Case: 
 
Nozzle Material Factor [frn]: 
 = min[Sn/S, 1] 
 = min[14788.8/37195.2, 1] 
 = 0.398 
 
Thickness of Nozzle [tn]: 
 = thickness - corrosion allowance 
 = 1.812 - 0.125 
 = 1.687 in. 
 
Shell Diameter to Thickness ratio [D/t]: 
 = Di/t 
 = 85.093/0.741 
 = 114.813 must be less than 400. 
 
Effective Pressure Radius [Reff]: 
 = Di/2 + corrosion allowance 
 = 84.843/2 + 0.125 
 = 42.546 in. 
 
Effective Length of Vessel Wall [LR]: 
 = min( sqrt( Reff * t ), 2 * Rn ) 
 = min( sqrt( 42.546 * 0.741 ), 2 * 10.313 ) 
 = 5.615 in. 
 
Thickness Limit Candidate [LH1]: 
 = min[1.5t,te] + sqrt( Rn * tn ) 
 = min[1.5* 0.741, 0.0] + sqrt( 10.313 * 1.687 ) 
 = 4.171 in. 
 
Thickness Limit Candidate [LH2]: 
 = Lpr1 
 = 11.811 
 = 11.811 in. 
 
Thickness Limit Candidate [LH3]: 
 = 8( t + te ) 
 = 8( 0.741 + 0.0 ) 
 = 5.929 in. 
 

[page 65]
PV Elite 2018 SP2 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 1950201-CAL-001-00 
Nozzle Calcs.: S2 
 
60 
Effective Nozzle Wall Length Outside the Vessel [LH]: 
 = min[ LH1, LH2, LH3 ] + t for set-in nozzles 
 = min[ 4.171, 11.811, 5.929 ) + 0.741 
 = 4.912 in. 
 
Effective Vessel Thickness [teff]: 
 = t + (( A5 * frp ) / LR ) 
 = 0.741+((0.0*1.0)/5.615) 
 = 0.741 in. 
 
Determine Parameter [Lamda]: 
 = min( 12, ( 2*Rn + tn )/( sqrt( ( Di + teff ) * teff )) ) 
 = min( 12, (2*10.31 + 1.687)/( sqrt((85.09 + 0.741) * 0.741)) ) 
 = 2.798 
 
Compute Areas A1-A43 (No Pad) or A1-A5 (With Pad) : 
 
Area Contributed by the Vessel Wall [A1]: 
 = t * LR * max( (Lamda/5)0.85, 1 ) 
 = 0.741 * 5.615 * max( (2.798/5)0.85, 1 ) 
 = 4.162 in² 
 
Area Contributed by the Nozzle Outside the Vessel Wall [A2]: 
 = tn * LH 
 = 1.687 * 4.912 
 = 8.287 in² 
 
Area Contributed by the Outside Fillet Weld [A41]: 
 = 0.5 * Leg412 
 = 0.5 * 0.3942 
 = 0.078 in² 
 
The total area contributed by A1 through A43 [AT]: 
 = A1 + frn( A2 + A3 ) + A41 + A42 + A43 
 = 4.162+0.398(8.287+0.0)+0.078+0.0+0.0 
 = 7.534 in² 
 
Nozzle Radius for Force Calculation [Rxn]: 
 = tn / ln[1 + tn/Rn ] 
 = 1.687/ln[ 1 + 1.687/10.313 ] 
 = 11.135 in. 
 
Shell Radius for Force Calculation [Rxs]: 
 = teff / ln[ 1 + teff/Reff ] 
 = 0.741/ln[ 1 + 0.741/42.546 ] 
 = 42.916 in. 
 
Allowable Local Primary Membrane Stress [Sallow]: 
 = 1.5 * S * E 
 = 1.5 * 37195.203 * 1.0 
 = 55792.8 psi 
 
Determine Force acting on the Nozzle [fN]: 
 = P * Rxn * LH 
 = 320.0 * 11.135 * 4.912 
 = 17503.6 lb. 
 
Determine Force acting on the Shell [fS]: 
 = P * Rxs( LR + tn ) 
 = 320.0 * 42.916( 5.615 + 1.687 ) 
 = 100284.1 lb. 
 
Discontinuity Force from Internal Pressure [fY]: 
 = P * Rxs * Rnc 
 = 320.0 * 42.916 * 10.313 
 = 141628.7 lb. 

[page 66]
PV Elite 2018 SP2 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 1950201-CAL-001-00 
Nozzle Calcs.: S2 
 
61 
 
Area Resisting Internal Pressure [Ap]: 
 = ( fS + fY + fN )/P 
 = ( 100284.1 + 141628.7 + 17503.6 )/320.0 
 = 810.7 in² 
 
Maximum Allowable Working Pressure Candidate [Pmax1]: 
 = Sallow /( 2 * Ap/AT - Rxs/teff ) 
 = 55792.805/( 2 * 810.676/7.534 - 42.916/0.741 ) 
 = 354.7 psig 
 
Maximum Allowable Working Pressure Candidate [Pmax2]: 
 = S[t/Rxs] 
 = 37195.203[ 0.741/42.916] 
 = 642.4 psig 
 
Maximum Allowable Working Pressure [Pmax]: 
 = min( Pmax1, Pmax2 ) 
 = min( 354.703, 642.35 ) 
 = 354.703 psig 
 
Average Primary Membrane Stress [SigmaAvg]: 
 = ( fN + fS + fY ) / AT 
 = ( 17503.613 + 100284.141 + 141628.672 )/7.534 
 = 34431.848 psi 
 
General Primary Membrane Stress [SigmaCirc]: 
 = P * Rxs / teff 
 = 320.0 * 42.916/0.741 
 = 18529.6 psi 
 
Maximum Local Primary Membrane Stress [PL]: 
 = max( 2 * SigmaAvg - SigmaCirc, SigmaCirc ) 
 = max( 2 * 34431.848 - 18529.551, 18529.551 ) 
 = 50334.1 psi

Strength of Nozzle Attachment Welds per 4.5.14 
 
Discontinuity Force Factor [ky]: 
 = ( Rnc + tn ) / Rnc 
 = ( 10.313 + 1.687 )/10.313 
 = 1.164 For set-in Nozzles 
 
Weld Length of Nozzle to Shell Weld [Ltau]: 
 = pi/2 * ( Rn + tn ) 
 = pi/2 * ( 10.313 + 1.687 ) 
 = 18.850 in. 
 
Weld Throat Dimensions, (0.7071*Leg Dimensions) [L41T, L42T, L43T]: 
 = 0.278, 0.000, 0.000, in. 
 
Required Weld Throat Dimensions : 
 tc, L41T = 0.278, must be >= min( 0.7 * 1.687, 0.250 ) Passed 
 
Weld Load Value [fwelds]: 
 = min( fy * ky, 1.5 * Sn( A2 + A3 ), pi/4*P*Rn^2*ky^2 ) 
 = min(141629*1.16,1.5*14788.8(8.287+0.0),pi/4*320.0*10.31^2*1.16^2) 
 = 36191.148 lb. 
 
Weld Stress Value [tau]: 
 = fwelds/(Ltau(0.49*L41T + 0.6*tw1 + 0.49*L43T ) ) 
 = 36191.148/(18.85(0.49* 0.278 + 0.6* 0.741 + 0.49*0.0 ) )

Intermediate Results: Saddle Reaction Q due to Wind or Seismic 
 
Saddle Reaction Force due to Wind Ft [Fwt]: 
 = Ftr * ( Ft/Num of Saddles + Z Force Load ) * B / E 
 = 3.0 * ( 23854.9/2 + 0 ) * 133.8976/84.8261 
 = 56482.4 lb. 
 
Saddle Reaction Force due to Wind Fl or Friction [Fwl]: 
 = max( Fl, Friction Load, Sum of X Forces) * B / Ls 
 = max( 1168.1, 101385.8, 0 ) * 133.8976/354.3307 
 = 38312.6 lb. 
 
Saddle Reaction Force due to Earthquake Fl or Friction [Fsl]: 
 = max( Fl, Friction Force, Sum of X Forces ) * B / Ls 
 = max( 71125.04, 101385.8, 0 ) * 133.8976/354.3307 
 = 38312.6 lb. 
 
Saddle Reaction Force due to Earthquake Ft [Fst]: 
 = Ftr * ( Ft/Num of Saddles + Z Force Load ) * B / E 
 = 3.0 * ( 71125/2 + 0 ) * 133.8976/84.8261 
 = 168405.8 lb. 
 
Load Combination Results for Q + Wind or Seismic [Q]: 
 = Saddle Load + Max( Fwl, Fwt, Fsl, Fst )

 = 0.0 (QO > QL --> No Uplift in Longitudinal direction)

 = 11.16 * 35562.52 + 0.0 
 = 396811.47 ft.lb.

 = Rmom / QO 
 = 4761738/339651.78 
 = 14.02 in. < Bplen/6 --> No Uplift in Transverse direction

 = max[0.0, 0.5095, 0.0]

 Value As = Sumof(A) - Ashell = 74.7683 in² 
 
 K1 = (1+cos(beta)-0.5*sin(beta)² )/(pi-beta+sin(beta)*cos(beta)) = 0.2035 
 
 Fh = K1 * Q = 0.2035 * 208948.641 = 42525.5781 lb. 
 
 Tension Stress, St = ( Fh/As ) = 568.7650 psi 
 Allowed Stress, Sa = 0.6 * Yield Str = 22800.0000 psi 
 
Saddle Splitting Dimension [d]: 
 = B - R * sin( theta )/ theta 
 = 66.1 - 42.55 * sin( 1.0472 )/1.0472 
 = 30.917 in. 
 
 Bending Moment, M = Fh * d = 109563.2188 ft.lb. 
 
 Bending Stress, Sb = ( M * C1 / I ) = 1763.8441 psi 
 Allowed Stress, Sa = 2/3 * Yield Str = 25333.3340 psi 
 
Minimum Thickness of Baseplate per Moss: 
 = ( 3( Q + Saddle_Wt )BasePlateWidth / ( 4 * BasePlateLength * AllStress ))½ 
 = ( 3(208949 + 3231)19.69/( 4 * 78.346 * 25333.334 ))½ 
 = 1.256 in.
